6 MODULE mode_lima_read_xker_raccs
7  IMPLICIT NONE
8 CONTAINS
9 ! ##########################################################################
10  SUBROUTINE lima_read_xker_raccs (KACCLBDAS,KACCLBDAR,KND, &
11  PALPHAS,PNUS,PALPHAR,PNUR,PESR,PBS,PBR,PCS,PDS,PFVELOS,PCR,PDR, &

14 ! ##########################################################################
15 !
16 !!**** * * - initialize the kernels for the rain-snow accretion process
17 !!
18 !! PURPOSE
19 !! -------
20 !! The purpose of this routine is to initialize the kernels PKER_RACCSS,
21 !! PKER_RACCS and PKER_SACCRG prepared from a previous run of the routine
22 !! INI_RAIN_ICE. The reading of the kernels is optional after checking for
23 !! the dimensions of the arrays.
24 !!
25 !!** METHOD
26 !! ------
27 !!
28 !!
29 !! EXTERNAL
30 !! --------
31 !! None
32 !!
33 !!
34 !! IMPLICIT ARGUMENTS
35 !! ------------------
36 !! None
37 !!
38 !! REFERENCE
39 !! ---------
40 !! Book2 of documentation ( routine READ_XKER_RACCS )
41 !!
42 !! AUTHOR
43 !! ------
44 !! J.-P. Pinty * Laboratoire d'Aerologie*
45 !!
46 !! MODIFICATIONS
47 !! -------------
48 !! Original 09/04/96
49 !!
50 !-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
51 !
52 !* 0. DECLARATIONS
53 ! ------------
54 !
55 !* 0.2 Declarations of local variables :
56 !
57 !
58 INTEGER, INTENT(OUT) :: KND,KACCLBDAS,KACCLBDAR
59 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PALPHAS
60 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PNUS
61 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PALPHAR
62 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PNUR
63 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PESR
64 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PBS
65 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PBR
